border-box;">整个比赛分为多个赛段进行，其中淘汰赛段的最后一名出局，最终冠军可以获得100万美元的奖金。比赛起点与终点均在美国，中间经过世界多个国家。各队必须按摄制组给出的路线资讯指引周游世界，并在赛程中完成规定的任务。</span></span></strong></p></section></section></section><section I like that one a lot because it's kind of true.</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 60px;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 40px;margin: 5px 10px;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.9984375" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKfVjSb4NaSmadz0wMb3r5rKWpZCtPZBqEgDgvSYgLV4uwjYLs3AIdc1DXNQibZOvuxia96iaicp2R5kHg/640?wx_fmt=jpegwebp" data-type="jpegwebp" data-w="640" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section><section style="font-size: 11px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Gwen</p></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;width: 75%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="vertical-align: top;margin-top: 29px;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;background-color: rgb(255, 228, 200);box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.85" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/pHY6GIbVTawth5QwMMSgkQ4p36aQKrMpcTlGHmfEDAYfEpQFqjhx9VD1wZNNGKlUOia0Xv699yPjw0D76ibXzD6g/640?wx_fmt=png?x-oss-process=style/xmwebp" data-type="png?x-oss-process=style/xmwebp" data-w="20" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section><section style="display: inline-block;width: 85%;margin-top: 11px;border-radius: 16px;background-color: rgb(255, 228, 200);padding: 16px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> It's like in Instagram. data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/xeicFry6DLQWLRlmP34CzicZ8Ots1Qs99426OPXk0tKgntt2gnP2weiaxBibxJ7iaNy0kh6C1IQW1YQwia8QX791vESQ/640?wx_fmt=gif" data-type="gif" data-w="640" style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(114, 114, 114);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;padding: 0px 5px 4px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 1.2em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Clearheaded  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj.（尤指在困境中）头脑清醒的，明白事理的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He was clear-headed enough to realize he was not particularly talented.  他清楚的意识到他没有特殊的天赋。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Pee </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">排尿（urinate的非正式说法），小便</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Prone   adj.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1、俯卧的，趴着的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The photograph showed a man lying prone on the pavement, a puddle of blood around his head.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这张照片上一名男子趴在人行道上，头部周围有一滩血。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2、易于遭受（疾病）的；有（消极）倾向的;</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">常用于be prone to sth/do sth 这个搭配</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He was prone to depression even as a teenager.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">甚至在青少年时期他就容易情绪抑郁。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">-prone 还可以做后缀，表示：较常碰到…问题的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">accident-prone易出事故的          injury-prone易受伤的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Fall for sth对…信以为真</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He told me that he owned a mansion in Spain and I fell for it.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他告诉我他在西班牙有一座庄园，我信以为真。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Fall for sb 对…倾心，迷恋…</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He's fallen for her in a big way.他完全被她迷住了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">hype  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.（新闻媒体的）大肆宣传，炒作</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I've been put off reading the book by all the hype.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">所有的宣传炒作让我对这本书产生了反感。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">v.（通过新闻媒体）大肆宣传，炒作</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's being hyped as the musical event of the year.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">它正被炒作成年度音乐盛事。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">hype sb up  使（某人）兴奋，使（某人）激动</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I always feel hyped up before an exam. 我在考试之前总是很兴奋。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Pseudoscience    n. 伪科学</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Empowered    adj.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">自信的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's important that girls feel empowered and in control of what happens to them.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">获得授权的，被赋予权力的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The editor may not be empowered to negotiate a contract.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Bug</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">v. 使烦恼，使恼怒，装窃听器， </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 小虫子，故障，窃听器，小病</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">they keep your house safe from other bugs.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他保护你们的房子不受害虫侵害</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">There’s another bug, some else is listening.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他身上还有别的窃听器，有别人在监听</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Ingrained    </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj.根深蒂固的，深嵌并难以清除的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Carols are a deeply ingrained part of the English Christmas tradition.  颂歌是英国人圣诞传统根深蒂固的组成部分</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;margin-top: 1.15em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 6px;height: 6px;margin-top: -3px;border-radius: 100%;float: left;background-color: rgb(232, 181, 181);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="border-top: 1px solid rgb(232, 181, 181);width: 99.9%;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="text-align: right;margin: -1.1em 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-align: left;padding: 3px 10px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">第三步   认真校对，查缺补漏</p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px;padding-left: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 95%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-left: 1px solid rgb(249, 110, 87);height: 1.2em;box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="padding-bottom: 8px;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="clear: none;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.没有听出来的意群：可能包括连读或者省音,分析错误的原因并做笔记。</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(188, 132, 37);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">今日听写答案</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;color: rgba(122, 120, 124, 0.91);font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: It migh</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">, however, ma</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">ke</span></span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> you have to pee a lot.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">它不会让你的皮肤更亮，不会让你的头脑更清醒，也不会让你感觉更有活力。相反，它只会让你一天跑几十趟厕所。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">Many people don'</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> understand the biology behind their bodies. tha</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Finally, when a whole crowd of animals came rushing towards him, he turned and ran for his life. And now anyone could see that the air of that young world was really doing the old gentleman good. In London he had been far too old to run: now, he ran at a speed which would have made him certain to win the hundred yards' race at any Prep school in England. His coattails flying out behind him were a fine sight. But of course it was no use.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">最后，当一大群动物朝他跑去时，他转身逃命去了。任何人都看得出，年轻世界的空气确实对这老先生大有裨益。在伦敦，他已经老得跑不动了，而现在，他的速度完全能拿下英格兰仔何一个预备学校百米赛的冠军。他的衣摆在身后飘来荡去，十分好看。但当然毫无用处。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 晚餐出去吃，然后去看电影吧。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 等一下！我无法同时付这两笔钱。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 别担心，我有钱。我请你。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 啊！你真好！</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: We're going out to dinner and then to the movies.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Hold on! I can't afford to pay for both.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Don't worry. I've got money. It's my treat.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Gee, that's really nice of you.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The preacher's ___________ voice put me to sleep.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">传教士单调的声音催我入眠。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">monotonous</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">汉译英</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">中国特色社会主义进入新时代，适应国际形势深刻复杂变化、党和国家事业快速发展的需要，立法工作进入了一个加快发展的新阶段，呈现覆盖广、数量多、节奏快、要求高的新特点。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">In this new era of socialism with Chinese characteristics, in response to the profound and complex changes in the international landscape and the rapid development of the cause of the Party and the country, our legislative work moved into a new stage of accelerated development, marked by a large volume of expedited and higher-standard legislation that covers a wide range of areas.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p style='text-align: center;outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: style="margin-top: 0.3em;padding-bottom: 1em;background-color: rgba(151, 195, 123, 0.44);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-width: 0.2em;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(151, 195, 123, 0.44);display: inline-block;width: 100%;margin-top: -1em;margin-left: -1em;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="padding: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">It's not time to make a change.</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Just relax, take it easy.</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">今日发音练习重点：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1. no* time /t/音省略</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2. ma<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">ke a</span></strong></span>  辅元连读</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3. ta<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">ke it ea</span></strong></span>sy </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">easy /ˈ<span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">i:</span>z<span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">i</span>/ 中两个元音相同。后一个/i/发音时长较前面的/i:/更短，且在弱读音节中，需要弱读。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);text-align: left;margin: 20px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40%;border-width: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);padding: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1.  词链儿：It's time to XX   到了XX的时候了</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">⑴ It's time for + n. “该是（干）……的时候了。”</strong><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Boys and girls,<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"> It's time for </span></strong></em>class.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">同学们，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">该</strong>上课了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">⑵ It's time + (for sb.) to do sth.  “该是（某人）干……的时候了。”</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">It's time for</span></em></strong><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"> you </span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">to </span></em></strong>clean the classroom.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">该是</strong>你打扫教室<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">的时候了</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">It's time to</span></em></strong> go to school.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">该</strong>去上学了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">⑶ It's time + that clause 时，that可省略，time可由high/about修饰。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">从句中的谓语动词有两种形式：可用动词的过去式(be用were)；或者用should + 动词原形（should不能省略)。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">此句型为虚拟语气句型，表示“现在某人该做某事了”（含有该事早该去做而未做，现在去做似乎都为时已晚的意思）。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">It's time （that）</span></em></strong>we went to bed.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">该</strong>去睡觉了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">It's high time that</span></em></strong> the article <g style="box-sizing: border-box;">were </g>published.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">发表这篇文章是<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">适时的</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">It's time</span></em></strong> you <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">should </span></em></strong>do <g style="box-sizing: border-box;">cleaning</g>. （should不可省略）</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">该去</strong>打扫卫生了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. 词链儿：make a change 做出改变</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I think it's time for me to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">make a change</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我认为现在是我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">改变现状</strong>的好时机。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">拓展：make a difference 有影响/起作用</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I believed that I can <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">make a difference</span></em></strong> in this world.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我坚信世界一定会<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">因我而</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">不同</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. 词链儿：Just relax. 放轻松。</strong></p></section><section style="z-index: 101;transform: translate(350.547px, 2109.91px);-webkit-transform: translate(350.547px, 2109.91px);-moz-transform: translate(350.547px, 2109.91px);-o-transform: translate(350.547px, 2109.91px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;">2</section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.694" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKewhxlrMSJkb9nIrMugoJSpw2TgRBSia3lZaPoviat27ZPauJvtTFKdL4r4ZbF4KGXhABetib4Fw9dqA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="500" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">4. 词链儿：Take it easy. 别着急。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">!</span></em></strong> It's early, no need to run.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">Take it easy.</span></em></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">好，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">别急</strong>。<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section style="z-index: 2;transform: translate(350.547px, 2524.61px);-webkit-transform: translate(350.547px, 2524.61px);-moz-transform: translate(350.547px, 2524.61px);-o-transform: translate(350.547px, 2524.61px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;">在说到自己成功地搞了一个噱头的时候，Emily并没有用到success这个词，而是用的pull off这个表达。<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：We<strong border-box;">把车停在路边</strong>卖点吃的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: border-box;">在说到自己成功地搞了一个噱头的时候，Emily并没有用到success这个词，而是用的pull off这个表达。<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">说到pull off大家想到的可能是"停车”</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：We<strong border-box;">把车停在路边</strong>卖点吃的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: target="_blank">toast只跟面包有关系吗？</a></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgba(255, 164, 30, 0.55);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(140, 140, 140);line-height: 1.6;letter-spacing: 2px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">早读|<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">口语</strong>|阅读|翻译|听写</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">编辑|排版 Claire</span></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">图片均来源于网络</p></section></sectio</section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(114, 114, 114);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;padding: 0px 5px 4px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Nonsense </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/'nɒns(ə)ns/ US/'nɑnsɛns/  (n.)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">If you say that something spoken or written is nonsense, you mean that you consider it to be untrue or silly. 胡言乱语; 蠢话 [表不满]</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：Nonsense. I’d love to do it.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">胡说，我非常愿意——《绝望主妇第四季》</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Undervalue </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/ʌndə'væljuː/ US/ˌʌndɚ'vælju/   (vt.)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">If you undervalue something or someone, you fail to recognize how valuable or important they are. 低估…的价值</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：We must never undervalue freedom.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们决不可低估自由的价值。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Undervalued(adj.)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">不被重视的，低估价值的，估值贬低的（货币）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：Then, it looked 25% undervalued compared with the dollar; today, that has swelled to 51%.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">比索较美元贬值25%；今天比索暴增至51%。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Kidney  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/'kɪdnɪ/ US/'kɪdni/(n.) </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Your kidneys are the organs in your body that take waste matter from your blood and send it out of your body as urine. 肾脏</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：It's gonna make your kidneys shut down.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这个会让你的肾功能停止。——《瑞克和莫蒂第一季》</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Either </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/'aɪðə/ US/'iðɚ/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">①(adj.)both: both of two things两者都...</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：No senior officials from either side are involved.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">双方的高级官员都未参与其中。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">②(conj.)either...or 要么...要么...（表示几个可选项中只能选其一）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：Catch either, or ideally both, if you can</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">两者中任一方面都值得玩味，如果你能，也可以兼顾双方</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">③用于否定句中，表示”也”</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：That's okay. They don't trust you, either.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">没事儿。她们也不信任你。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Filter </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/'fɪltə/ US/'fɪltɚ/  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">①(n.)A filter is a device through which a substance is passed when it is being filtered. 过滤器</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：Be aware of your personal perceptual filters.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">要意识到自己的“感知过滤器”。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">②(v.) If light or sound filters into a place, it comes in weakly or slowly, either through a partly covered opening, or from a long distance away. (光、声) 透入</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：Sounds of cheering filtered in through the closed window.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">欢呼声透过关闭的窗户传了进来。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Do justice </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">treat or consider adequately or fairly公平对待</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：But the tales do not do you justice, my lady.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">但百闻不如一见 小姐——《权力的游戏 第二季》</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Fluid </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/'fluːɪd/ US/'fluɪd/    </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">①(n.)liquid: a liquid substance 液体</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：Ebola spreads through bodily fluids such as blood or saliva.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">埃博拉通过血液或唾液等体液传播。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">②(adj.)Fluid movements or lines or designs are smooth and graceful. 优雅流畅的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：Gestures in iOS 11 are more fluid.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">iOS 11操作系统的手势更加流畅。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Delicate </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/'delɪkət/ US/'dɛləkət/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">①(adj.)You use delicate to describe a situation, problem, matter, or discussion that needs to be dealt with carefully and sensitively.微妙的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：Now, we know it’s a delicate line to cross,but...</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们都知道这个界限有点微妙</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">②(adj.)If something is delicate, it is easy to harm, damage, or break, and needs to be handled or treated carefully. =fragile易碎的; 脆弱的；敏感的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：Does this offend your delicate sensibilities?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你那敏感的神经是不是受不了了？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Affect </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/ə'fekt/ US/ə'fɛkt/  (vt.)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">If something affects a person or thing, it influences them or causes them to change in some way.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> =(n.)have an effect on(某事物) 影响 (某人或物)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：whatever affects one directly affects all indirectly.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">任何直接影响到个体的东西都会间接影响到整体。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">        举个例子：Do video games have an effect on children’s behaviour?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">电子游戏对孩子的行为有影响吗？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;margin-top: 1.15em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 6px;height: 6px;margin-top: -3px;border-radius: 100%;float: left;background-color: rgb(232, 181, 181);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="border-top: 1px solid rgb(232, 181, 181);width: 99.9%;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="text-align: right;margin: -1.1em 0px border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">第三步   认真校对，查缺补漏</p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">In a very few minutes some of them got ahead of him. They lined up in a row and barred his way. Others hemmed him in from behind. Wherever he looked he saw terrors. Antlers of great elks and the huge face of an elephant towered over him. Heavy, serious-minded bears and boars grunted behind him. Cool-looking leopards and panthers with sarcastic faces (as he thought) stared at him and waved their tails. What struck him most of all was the number of open mouths. The animals had really opened their mouths to pant; he thought they had opened their mouths to eat him. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">几分钟后，一些动物就超过了他。它们排起来断了他的去路，其他动物从后面追上将他包围。他无论从哪个方向看去，都感到可怕极了大麋子的角和大象庞大的脸高耸在他面前。那些笨重而严肃的熊和公野猪在后面咆哮。表情冷漠的黑豹和花豹讥讽地（他这么想）摇着尾巴，盯着他。最令他心惊肉跳的是那么多张大的嘴。动物们张口是为了喘气，他却认为是要吃他。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 你会说英语吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 会一点。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 你能告诉我玉佛寺怎么走吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 对不起，我听不懂你的话。请你说得慢一点行吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Do you speak English?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Yes, a little.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Can you tell me how to get to the Jade Buddha Temple?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I'm sorry. I can't quite follow you. Would you mind speaking slowly?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The horse _____________ at the sound of the explosion.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">马听到爆炸声受了惊。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">took a fright</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">汉译英</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">民法典是新中国成立以来第一部以“法典”命名的法律，是中国特色社会主义法律体系中固根本、稳预期、利长远的基础性法律。常委会认真做好民法典实施准备工作，推动相关配套法规和司法解释的修改完善，阐释好民法典一系列新规定新概念新精神，带头做好宣传、推进、保障实施工作，让民法典走到群众身边、走进人民心里。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The Civil Code is the first piece of legislation to carry the title of code that has been enacted since the founding of the People's Republic of China. The Code is a fundamental law in the socialist system of laws with Chinese characteristics that serves to build the legal foundation, stabilize expectations, and yield long-term benefits. The Standing Committee made effective preparations for its implementation and pushed for revisions and improvements to supporting laws, regulations, and judicial interpretations. We thoroughly explained the new regulations, concepts, and principles in the Civil Code, and led the way in publicizing, promoting, and ensuring its implementation, so that this law is thoroughly observed throughout society and well received by the people.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: transparent;padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(17, 1, 1);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Hormone  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Noun  /ˈhɔːr.moʊn/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：any of various chemicals made by living cells that influence the</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">development, growth, sex, etc. of an animal and are carried around the body in the blood荷尔蒙，激素</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">male and female hormones</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">雄性和雌性激素</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">fluid  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">noun /ˈfluː.ɪd/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：a substance that flows and is not solid液体；流质</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">If you have a fever you should drink plenty of fluids.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">如果发烧，应多喝流质。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Adjective   /ˈfluː.ɪd/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：smooth and continuous流畅的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">fluid movements</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">流畅的动作</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：If situations, ideas, or plans are fluid, they are not fixed and are</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> likely to change, often repeatedly and unexpectedly.（情况、想法或计划）不固定的，易变的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The military situation is still very fluid.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">军事局势依然很不稳定。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">substance</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">noun /ˈsʌb.stəns/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：material with particular physical characteristics物质；材料</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">an organic/chemical substance</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有机／化学物质</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：importance, seriousness, or relationship to real facts重要性；要旨；实质；根据</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">There is no substance in the allegation.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这项指控毫无根据。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">illegal substance </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：an illegal drug毒品</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：the most important part of what someone has said or written（某人）所说（或所写）的最重要的部分，要点</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Later that year, the substance of their secret conversation appeared in a newspaper article.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">那年稍后，他们这次秘密谈话的要点出现在报纸上的一篇文章中。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">structure</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">noun  /ˈstrʌk.tʃər/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：the way in which the parts of a system or object are arranged or</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">organized, or a system arranged in this way结构；构造；机构；体系</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the grammatical structure of a sentence</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">句子的语法结构</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：something that has been made or built from parts, especially</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a large building结构体；（尤指）大型建筑物</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The proposed new office tower is a steel and glass structure 43 storeys high.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">拟议建造的新办公大楼是一栋高43层的钢铁玻璃结构的建筑物。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：an organ in the body, or part of an organ, that does a particular job（器官的）结构</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Verb</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to plan, organize, or arrange the parts of something构成；组织</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We must carefully structure and rehearse each scene.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们每一场戏都必须认真构思、认真排练。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">nephron</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">noun  /ˈnef.rɒn/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：a basic unit of the kidney肾元，肾单位</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The kidneys contain millions of tiny filtering units called nephrons.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">肾脏中含有几百万个被称为肾元的过滤单位。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">conveyor belt</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">noun  /kənˈveɪ.ɚ ˌbelt/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：a continuous moving strip or surface that is used for transporting</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> objects from one place to another传送带，传输带</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Sodium </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Noun   /ˈsəʊ.di.əm/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：a soft, silver-white chemical element that is found in salt钠</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Glucose</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Noun   /ˈɡluː.kəʊs/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：a type of sugar that is found in plants, especially fruit, and</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">supplies an important part of the energy that animals need（植物、尤指水果中的）葡萄糖</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">calcium</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">noun   /ˈkæl.si.əm/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：a chemical element that is present in teeth, bones, and chalk（化学元素）钙</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">amino acid</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">noun   /əˌmiː.nəʊ ˈæs.ɪd/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：any of the chemical substances found in plants and animals that</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">combine to make protein (= a substance necessary for the body to grow)氨基酸，胺酸</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">homeostasis</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">noun  /ˌhəʊ.mi.əʊˈsteɪ.sɪs/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：the ability or tendency of a living organism, cell, or group to keep the conditions inside it the same despite any changes in the conditions around it, or this state of internal balance体内动态平衡（机体、活细胞、组织等，在其外部环境变化的情况下，保持内部不变或平衡状态的能力或趋向）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Warm-blooded animals are able to achieve temperature homeostasis.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">热血动物能够实现体温平衡。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Bladder </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Noun /ˈblæd.ər/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：an organ like a bag inside the body of a person or animal, where urine is stored before it leaves the body膀胱</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">to empty your bladder (= urinate)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">撒尿</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">urine</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">noun /ˈjʊə.rɪn/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：the yellowish liquid waste that is released from the body when you urinate尿液，小便</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">fit in</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to feel that you belong to a particular group and are accepted by that group合得来；适应</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's no surprise she's leaving - she never really fitted in.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她要离开——这一点也不意外，因为她从来都没有真正融入过。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：If one thing fits in with another thing, they look pleasant together or are suitable for each other.相合；合适</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's a very nice sofa but it doesn't fit in with the rest of the room.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这个沙发很漂亮，但是跟房间里其他的家具不搭配。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">fit sb/sth in</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to find time to do or deal with something or someone找时间做（或处理）；安排时间见（某人）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Dr Jones is very busy but I'm sure she'll be able to fit you in tomorrow.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">琼斯医生很忙，但是我肯定她明天能安排时间见您。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">fit the bill</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> 英文释义：to be suitable for a particular purpose与目的相符</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">This new software fits the bill.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这款新软件肯定符合要求。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">fit to be tied</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：extremely angry极其生气，怒不可遏</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">fit to burst</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：If someone is fit to burst with an emotion or a feeling, it is very strong inside them.充满（某种情绪、感情）的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The children were fit to burst with excitement.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">孩子们都兴奋极了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">fit to drop</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：extremely tired极度疲劳，非常累</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">After the run they were fit to drop.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">跑完之后，他们累趴下了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.没有听出来的意群：可能包括连读或者省音,分析错误的原因并做笔记。</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">今日听写答案</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;color: rgba(122, 120, 124, 0.91);font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">（请务必听写后校对） </span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">红色连读</span><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">；<span style="color: rgba(46, 159, 238, 0.863);box-sizing: border-box;">蓝色爆破省读</span>；<span style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);box-sizing: border-box;">橙色弱读 <span style="font-size: 14px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">如果任何物质的含量过高或过低，那都是有害的。肾脏的工作就是将这些物质的水平保持在正确的区域。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: They don't.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">那么，一天八杯水能起到什么作用呢？没有作用。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">"I object to that remark very strongly," said the Bulldog. But the Elephant walked quietly to the river, filled her trunk with water, and came back to attend to Uncle Andrew. The sagacious animal went on doing this till gallons of water had been squirted over him, and water was running out of the skirts of his frock-coat as if he had been for a bath with all his clothes on. In the end it revived him. He awoke from his faint. What a wake it was! But we must leave him to think over his wicked deed (if he was likely to do anything so sensible) and turn to more important things.   </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“我强烈反对。”公狗说。但大象默默地走到河边，用鼻子灌满水，回来洒在安德鲁舅舅身上。这有灵性的动物不断地浇，直到好多好多水浇到他身上，又从他外衣的边缘流了出来，犹如他穿着衣服洗了一次澡。最后，他恢复了理智，从昏迷中醒了过来，彻彻底底地清醒了！但我们必须将他撇开，让他慢慢去想他做过的坏事(如果他还有可能做出如此有理智的事的话)，我们去讲些更重要的事情。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 我不相信你婚礼时天气会那么好。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 是啊，太完美了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 还有所有的花都盛开着。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我不能要求更多了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I can't believe the weather is so gorgeous for your wedding.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Yes, It's perfect.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: And all of the flowers are in bloom.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I couldn't have asked for more.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">That hairstyle is as dead as a dodo now.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">那种发型早就________了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">过时</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">汉译英</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">一条1万3英里的土石之龙蜿蜒于中国乡野之间，它的历史几乎与其结构一样悠久曲折。城墙起于西部临洮，止于东部辽东，合在一起称为长城。长城最初是多座泥土夯实的城墙，由春秋战国时期的各个独立封建国家修筑，以抵制中国北方游牧民和其它国家。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A 13,000 mile dragon of earth and stone winds its way through the countryside of China with a history almost as long and serpentine as the structure. As the structures grew from Lintao in the west to Liaodong in the east, they collectively became known as The Great Wall. The Great Wall began as multiple walls of rammed earth built by individual feudal states during the Chunqiu period to protect against nomadic raiders north of China and each other.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p style='text-align: center;outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 0.544px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;'><strong style="outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;box-sizing: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. Mountain Climbing Day → 登高：古有重阳节登高的风俗。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">the Double Ninth Festival  重阳节</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 14px;">九月九日：即重阳节。古以九为阳数，故曰重阳。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 14px;">忆：想念。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 14px;">山东：王维本太原祁人，后迁居于蒲（今山西永济），蒲州在函谷关与华山以东，所以称山东。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>3.</strong> <a data-linktype="2" href="https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653549254&amp;idx=1&amp;sn=34639050e9306db52f20d51711110132&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="点击链接跳转回顾【词汇辨析：alone &amp; lone &amp; lonely】"><strong>点击链接跳转回顾【词汇辨析：alone &amp; lone &amp; lonely】</strong></a><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">两个“异”字，一个“独”字：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">独--alone （独自，但无“孤独”之意）</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">异乡--a foreign land</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">异客--a lonely stranger（lonely adj. 孤单的，寂寞的）</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">4. foreign land 异国他乡</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He took a plane across the sea to some <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">foreign land</span></strong></em>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他乘坐飞机漂洋过海去了一个<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">陌生的国度</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">5. </strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">double adj. 成对的；双倍的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">doubly adv. 加倍地；由于双重原因</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: border-box;">doubly</span></em></strong> difficult/hard/important <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">越发</strong>困难╱努力╱重要</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I made<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"> doubly</span></em></strong> sure I locked all the doors when I went out.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">一再</strong>查看所有的门都锁好后才出门。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">In pregnancy, a high fibre diet is <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">doubly</span></em></strong> important.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">怀孕期间高纤维饮食<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">倍加</strong>重要。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Well, then you should consider this visit <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">doubly</span></em></strong> disappointing.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">那你就该明白这次拜访令人失望<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">至极</strong>。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align:
