powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;">怀念；苦苦思念；渴望得到...</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">After two months in France, I was <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">pining for</span></em></strong> home.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在法国待了两个月后，我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">盼望着</strong>回家。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He's still <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">pining for</span></em></strong> his ex-girlfriend.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他还在<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">苦苦思念着</strong>他的前女友。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>We don't <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">pine for</span></em></strong> the past. We don't fear the future. We grab for it.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们不<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">留恋</strong>过去。我们不惧怕未来。我们要抓住它（机遇）。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>I definitely will <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">pine for</span></em></strong> some chocolate.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我一定会<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">想</strong>吃巧克力的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Do not despair, nor <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">pine for</span></em></strong> my safe return.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">不要绝望，也不要<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">渴望</strong>我的平安归来。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">7. kinsfolk noun. 亲戚，家人；亲属</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">kinsfolk 也可直接表达为：kin</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">拓展表达：next of kin=your most closely related family </strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">最近的亲属，直系亲属</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">One of the drivers was fatally injured; his <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">next of kin</span></em></strong> has been informed.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">其中一名司机受了致命伤，已通知了他的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">最近亲</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">8. with dogwood spray in hand 插入语</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I know my brothers would climb up mountain and miss me so far away.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">远在故乡的兄弟们今天登高时身上都佩上了茱萸，却发现少了一位兄弟──自己不在内。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">→ dogwood n. 山茱萸； 梾木；梾木的木材</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 14px;">茱萸（zhū yú）：即草决明，一名越椒，芳香植物。古时人们认为重阳节插戴茱萸可以避灾克邪。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">→ spray n. （用作装饰的）小树枝，小花枝</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">All the wedding guests wore <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">sprays</span></em></strong> of carnations.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">所有参加婚礼的来宾都戴着<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">小枝</strong>康乃馨。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: justify;font-size: 14px;line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">大家找到这个表达了吗？有没有觉得，原来好简单啊？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;">词链</span></strong><span style="letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;">：XX be gonna be in good hands XX有指望了；XX会被照顾的很好；XX指日可待</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句1</span></strong><span style="letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;">：</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I know the most about your case. I promise<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> you will be in very good hands</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我最了解你的情况。我保证<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">你能得到很好的照料</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句2：</span></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I want you to know, <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">you're gonna be in good hands</strong>. I've been doing this for a long time.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有我在<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">你放心</strong>，我是老手了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句3：</span></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">As you can see, <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">I'm in good hands</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你可以看到，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">我情况良好</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句4：</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You are <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">in such good hands with Phil</strong>. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">菲尔<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">帮你们干得不错嘛。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">大家学会了吗？下面我们再来多学习几个跟hand有关的词链吧。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section 144);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">all hands on deck 总动员；全民皆兵</strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：There are 30 people coming to dinner tonight, so it's <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">all hands on deck</strong>. 今天晚上有 30 人来吃饭，要<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">全体动员</strong>了。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">get your hands dirty 做体力活</strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">getting his hands dirty</strong>. 他不怕体力劳动。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">have your hands full 忙得不可开交</strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</strong>She certainly<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> has her hands full</strong> with four kids in the house. 家里养着四个孩子，她当然<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">忙得团团转</strong>。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: border-box;">以免技巧生疏</strong>。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;">词链</span></strong><span style="letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;">：XX be gonna be in good hands XX有指望了；XX会被照顾的很好；XX指日可待</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句1</span></strong><span style="letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;">：</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I know the most about your case. I promise<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> you will be in very good hands</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我最了解你的情况。我保证<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">你能得到很好的照料</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句2：</span></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I want you to know, <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">you're gonna be in good hands</strong>. I've been doing this for a long time.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有我在<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">你放心</strong>，我是老手了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句3：</span></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">As you can see, <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">I'm in good hands</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你可以看到，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">我情况良好</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句4：</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You are <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">in such good hands with Phil</strong>. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">菲尔<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">帮你们干得不错嘛。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">大家学会了吗？下面我们再来多学习几个跟hand有关的词链吧。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="padding: 3px;display: inline-block;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(251, 152, 144);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">all hands on deck 总动员；全民皆兵</strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：There are 30 people coming to dinner tonight, so it's <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">all hands on deck</strong>. 今天晚上有 30 人来吃饭，要<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">全体动员</strong>了。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="padding: 3px;display: inline-block;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(251, 152, 144);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">get your hands dirty 做体力活</strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：He's not frightened of <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">getting his hands dirty</strong>. 他不怕体力劳动。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.5611814" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKcLmypm2OlKY1eIYxibSk1u9zzzaYLnKiaCqbqTuQ1CsVdEyRd2v1axOIPxdYfH3t07jvkoy9KqE4cA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="474" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="padding: 3px;display: inline-block;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(251, 152, 144);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">have your hands full 忙得不可开交</strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</strong>She certainly<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> has her hands full</strong> with four kids in the house. 家里养着四个孩子，她当然<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">忙得团团转</strong>。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="padding: 3px;display: inline-block;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(251, 152, 144);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">keep your hand in 保持熟练</strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：She retired last year but still teaches the odd class to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">keep her hand in</strong>. 她去年退休了，但偶尔还上课，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">以免技巧生疏</strong>。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 1.2em solid style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: transparent;padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(17, 1, 1);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Sweat </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ swet; swɛt /出汗，流汗，冒汗</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I was sweating a lot despite the air conditioning.尽管开着空调，我仍是满头大汗。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">辛苦工作，拼命干活</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">They sweated and saved for ten years to buy a house. 他们拼命工作，攒十年钱买了一栋房子。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Volume </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ‘vɒljuːm; ˋvɑljəm /音量，响度</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Can you turn the volume up?请你把音量调大好吗？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">总量</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The volume of trade贸易量</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Compensate </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/kɒmpənseɪt; ˋkɑmpən͵set /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">to replace or balance the effect of something bad弥补，补偿</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Because my left eye is so weak, my right eye has to work harder to compensate.因为我左眼视力差，右眼就要辛苦点来弥补一下。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">To pay someone money because they suffered injury, loss or damage</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The government’s promise to compensate victims of the flood政府对水灾灾民给予补偿的许诺</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Absorb</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">to take in liquid, gas, or another substance from the surface or space around something吸收</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Plants avsorb nutrients from the soil.植物从土壤中吸收养分</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">理解，吸收</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Her capacity to absorb information is amazing.她吸收信息的能力令人惊奇。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">使……全神贯注，吸引某人</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The movement and noise of the machines absorbed him completely.机器的运转和声响把它完全吸引住了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Sense </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ sens; sɛns /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">感觉到，意识到</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Perhaps he sensed your distrust.也许他感觉到了你的不信任。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Signal </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈsɪɡnəl/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">发信号，打信号，示意</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She signaled, and the waiter brought the bill.她打了个收拾，侍者就拿来了账单。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">标示着，预示</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The lengthening days that signal the end of winter白昼变长标志着冬天的结束</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Dehydration </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˌdiːhaɪˈdreɪʃən/ 脱水</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Dehydrate使脱水，使干燥the substance is dehydrated and stored as powder.该物质经脱水处理后以粉末形式储存。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Dehydrated脱水的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Instinct </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈɪnstɪŋkt/本能，直觉，天性</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Animals have a natural instinct for survival.动物有求生的自然本能。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Aslan threw up his shaggy head, opened his mouth, and uttered a long, single note; not very loud, but full of power. Polly's heart jumped in her body when she heard it. She felt sure that it was a call, and that anyone who heard that call would want to obey it and (what's more) would be able to obey it, however many worlds and ages lay between. And so, though she was filled with wonder, she was not really astonished or shocked when all of a sudden a young woman, with a kind, honest face stepped out of nowhere and stood beside her.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">阿斯兰昂起多毛的头，张口呼出长长的、不很嘹亮但有力的一声。波莉听得心跳加快。她敢肯定，那是一种呼唤，任何人听到这声呼唤，不管隔了多少世界多少年代，都想听从而且都能够听从。虽然她心中充满了好奇，但当一个看上去善良、诚实的年轻女人不知从哪儿走出来站在她旁边时，她并没有被吓一跳或者感到十分震惊。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 糟了！快迟到了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 要我帮忙吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 要，如果你能开车送我进城，我会感激不尽。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 没问题！反正我有时间。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Oh, no! Now I'll be late.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Can I give you a hand?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Yes, I'd appreciate it if you could drive me downtown.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Sure thing. I've got time.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I heard the news on the grapevine.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我是 __________ 知道的新闻。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">道听途说</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">汉译英</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">总的看，虽然挑战前所未有，更具有复杂性、全局性，但机遇也前所未有，更具有战略性、可塑性，机遇大于挑战，我国有中国共产党领导和中国特色社会主义制度的显著优势，经济长期向好的趋势没有改变，我国发展仍处于重要战略机遇期。我们有信心、有底气、有能力危中寻机、化危为机，不断开创我国经济社会发展的新局面。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Overall, although we face unprecedented and significant challenges of ever greater complexity, we are also presented with unprecedentedly promising strategic opportunities, and there are more opportunities than challenges. China possesses the notable strengths of the CPC's leadership and its system of socialism with Chinese characteristics. Our economy's long-term positive momentum remains unchanged, and our country is still in an important period of strategic opportunity for development. We have the confidence, foundation, and ability to seek opportunities amid crises and turn challenges into opportunities, and thus to continue to open up new prospects for China's economic and social development.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p style='text-align: center;outline: 0px;max-width: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">People are attracted to people with talent. People without it find that threatening. </strong></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">今日发音练习重点：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1. attract和talent都包含元音/æ/；</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2. threatening /ˈθretn-ɪŋ/ -ten可以发鼻爆/tn/；也可以发/tən/；</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3. 本句中that为指示性代词，不弱读。<br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);text-align: left;margin: 20px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40%;border-width: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);padding: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. 词链儿：be attracted to XX 爱慕XX，为XX所吸引</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I'm <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">attracted to</span></strong></em> warm, earthy colours.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">被</strong>温暖的土色<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">吸引住了</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He was nice looking, but I wasn't deeply <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">attracted to</span></em></strong> him.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他长得挺好看，但我并没有被他深深<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">吸引</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>Others <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">are attracted to</span></em></strong> me because of my positive energy.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">别人<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">被</strong>我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">吸引</strong>是因为我的正能量。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>Why <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">are</span></em></strong> we <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">attracted to</span></em></strong> some things?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">为什么我们会<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">被</strong>某些东西<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">吸引</strong>？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You can't always help who you're <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">attracted to</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有时候人们就是会控制不住<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">喜欢上</strong>谁。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.6037037" not <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">be attracted to</span></em></strong> me?</p><p border-box;">图源《特种部队》</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. people with talent = talented people 有天赋的人</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">People without it (it=talent) → 没有天赋/没有才能的人 → 平庸之辈</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Those who are so-called <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">unsuccessful </span></em></strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">people with talent</span></em></strong> are devoid of ability.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">那些所谓<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">怀才不遇的人</strong>，实际上还是缺乏能力。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. find sb/sth + adj.  发现，发觉；认为；（处于某状态、在做某事）</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">found </span></em></strong>the beds very <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">comfortable</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">发现</strong>这些床非常<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">舒适</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You may <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">find it hard</span></em></strong> to accept your illness.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你可能<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">觉得难以</strong>相信自己患病。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">4. threaten v. 威胁，恐吓</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">→ threatening adj.〔行为〕带有威胁的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">threatening</span></em></strong> gesture</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">一个<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">威胁的</strong>手势</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">threatening</span></em></strong> letters</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">恐吓</strong>信</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: How?<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">I</strong>: How do you think? Catherine broke into my room.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">R</strong>: I told you to destroy those years ago. Why you keep them?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">I</strong>: You know, for the memories.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">R</strong>: You kept them for insurance. You were scared I wouldn't give you the money I promised when Carlo died. You didn't trust me.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">I</strong>: How could I? You lie all the time. To your husband, your lovers, to everyone. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">R</strong>: If Catherine has the letters, how long before she finds out what we did in Galveson? You, you have ruined us.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I: You're the one with poison in her purse.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">R: How many times do I have to tell you <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">I was framed</strong>？Any theories on who would have done something like that?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I: So that's your next move. You're going to try to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">pin this on me</strong>?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">R: All I know is I didn't do it.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I: Well, neither did I. I got to get the hell out of Dodge.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">R</strong>: The ingratitude. I give you a home, a job.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">I</strong>: A job as a maid. We're blood. 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: none;box-sizing: border-box;">例句</span></strong><span style="text-decoration: none;box-sizing: border-box;">：</span><span style="text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;">Luckily, Sputnik<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> sticks around</strong> to help. </span><span style="text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;">幸运的是，Sputnik<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">留下来</strong>帮助了它。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></span></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">leave XX to rot 让XX自生自灭</strong></span></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: none;box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</span></strong><span style="text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;">You wanna just<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> leave me to rot </strong>in an alley somewhere? </span><span style="text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;">你想把我丢在路边让我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">自生自灭</strong>吗？</span></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">be on to XX 针对XX；找XX的茬</strong></span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：Her husband found that she had a lover and was <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">on to her</strong>. 她丈夫发现她有个情人，正在<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">调查她</strong>。<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">clean up the mess  收拾烂摊子</strong></span></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: none;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</strong>I am tired of<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> cleaning up the mess</strong> you made. 我受够了给你<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">收拾烂摊子</strong>了。</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;padding: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0% 5px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">R</strong>: She found my letters? How?<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">I</strong>: How do you think? Catherine broke into my room.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">R</strong>: I told you to destroy those years ago. Why you keep them?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">I</strong>: You know, for the memories.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">R</strong>: You kept them for insurance. You were scared I wouldn't give you the money I promised when Carlo died. You didn't trust me.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">I</strong>: How could I? You lie all the time. To your husband, your lovers, to everyone. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">R</strong>: If Catherine has the letters, how long before she finds out what we did in Galveson? You, you have ruined us.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I: You're the one with poison in her purse.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">R: How many times do I have to tell you <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">I was framed</strong>？Any theories on who would have done something like that?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I: So that's your next move. You're going to try to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">pin this on me</strong>?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">R: All I know is I didn't do it.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I: Well, neither did I. And you know what? I ain't <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">sticking around to </strong>find out who did.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">R: Meaning what?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">I</strong>: Tomorrow I'm buying a bus ticket for parts unknown.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">R</strong>: What, you're just going  to<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> leave me here to rot</strong>?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">I</strong>: Catherine<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">'s on to </strong>us. I got to get the hell out of Dodge.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">R</strong>: The ingratitude. I give you a home, a job.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">I</strong>: A job as a maid. We're blood. And somewhere along the way, you forgot that. Well I quit. This is <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">one mess you're going to have to clean up </strong>yourself.</p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;">be framed  被陷害；被诬陷</span></strong></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: none;box-sizing: border-box;">例句</span></strong><span style="text-decoration: none;box-sizing: border-box;">：He says he<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> was framed</strong>. 他说他是<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">被诬陷</strong>的。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 让XX自生自灭</strong></span></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: none;box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</span></strong><span style="text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;">You wanna just<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> leave me to rot </strong>in an alley somewhere? </span><span style="text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;">你想把我丢在路边让我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">自生自灭</strong>吗？</span></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">be on to XX 针对XX；找XX的茬</strong></span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：Her husband found that she had a lover and was <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">on to her</strong>. 她丈夫发现她有个情人，正在<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">调查她</strong>。<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我不想给你收拾烂摊子了，你自己在这自生自灭吧。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1. kidney </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈkɪdni/ n. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">one of the two organs in your lower back that separate waste products from your blood and make urine肾;肾脏;(食用的)动物腰子</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The hospital is trying to raise funds for a new kidney machine. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这家医院正设法募集资金购买一台新的血液透析器。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2. worn </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/wɔ:n $ wɔ:rn/ adj. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a worn object is old and damaged, especially because it has been used a lot穿坏的;用坏的;用旧的;磨薄的;疲惫的;筋疲力尽的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I am happy when I can relax my tense face muscles and my worn spirit in deep seriousness. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">当我那紧张的面部肌肉和疲惫的灵魂可以在深沉的严肃中得到松弛时，我才感到快乐。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3. miss </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/mɪs/ v. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">未击中;未得到;未达到;错过;未见到;未听到;未觉察;不理解;不懂;思念</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">miss the point 不得要领</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">There's value in the metric, but most people miss the point. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这项度量是有意义的，但很多人都没抓住重点。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4. granola </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/grəˈnəʊlə $ -ˈnoʊ-/n. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">格兰诺拉麦片(用烘烤过的谷类、坚果等配制成的早餐食品)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He likes snacks on granola doused with apple juice. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他喜欢将格兰诺拉麦片蘸上苹果汁来吃。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(255, 192, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">The </span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">answer’s simple: there is no ‘should’. When you feel thirsty, drink some water. You can trust your body.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">答案很简单：没有应不应该一说，觉得渴了就喝呗，你要信任自己的身体。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">Unless </span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">you </span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(255, 192, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">have </span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">kidney stones or </span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(255, 192, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">are</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> elderly -- sometimes, our messaging systems ge</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> little worn with age -- or your doctor has tol</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d you</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">, otherwise constantly monitoring how much water you drink is no</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> really necessary.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">除非你有肾结石或上了年纪</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">——</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">有时，我们的信息系统会随着年龄的增长而有些老化</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">——</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">或者你的医生告诉你（要持续监测），否则一直监测你喝了多少水其实不是很有必要。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">Here'</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> point that's often missed: every single thing you consume contains water.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">有一点经常被忽视：人摄入的每一样东西都含有水分。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">Your morning coffee has water. So doe</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s y</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">our breakfast.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">早上的咖啡里有水，早餐也有水。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">And that snack -- a</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">pple, an orange, a gla</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ss o</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">f juice, a granola bar -- jus</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> like you, they're ma</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">de o</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">f water too.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">而那些零食</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">——</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">苹果、橙子、果汁、一条格兰诺拉麦片棒</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">——</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">就像人一样，它们也是由水组成的。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">So as long as you're listening to your body's internal sen</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">se o</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">f thirst, there's really no nee</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> to be counting those eight glasses.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">所以只要听从自己身体内部对口渴的感觉，真的没有必要非得喝正好八杯水。</span></p><p style="line-height: 19px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Polly knew at once that it was the Cabby's wife, fetched out of our world not by any tiresome magic rings, but quickly, simply and sweetly as a bird flies to its nest. The young woman had apparently been in the middle of a washing day, for she wore an apron, her sleeves were rolled up to the elbow, and there were soapsuds on her hands. If she had had time to put on her good clothes (her best hat had imitation cherries on it) she would have looked dreadful; as it was, she looked rather nice.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">波莉立刻明白，那就是马车夫的妻子，不是被任何折磨人的魔法戒指从我们的世界硬生生地拖过去的，而是如鸟儿回巢一般迅捷、简单、舒适地到了那里。那年轻女人系着围裙，袖子挽到肘部，手上还沾着肥皂泡，显然刚才正在洗衣服。如果有时间换上好衣服(她最好的帽子上镶有樱桃饰)，她看上去准会让人讨厌。那身朴实无华的衣服却使她显得相当可爱。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 你带了我昨天借你的五块钱了吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 噢，我忘了。我会很快跑回家给你拿。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 你不必现在就去。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我不想你认为我懒得还你的钱。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Do you have the five dollars I lent you yesterday?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Oh, I forgot! I'll run home quickly and bring you the money.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: You don't have to go right away.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I'd hate for you to think I was lazy in returning your money.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">They paid a king's ransom for the painting.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他们为这幅画___________。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">花了大价钱</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">汉译英</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">没有哪一代人比你们拥有更强大的力量，没有哪一代人比你们能够更快的做出改变。我们现在实现目标的速度已经大幅缩短，在科技的帮助下，每个人都可以通过工具、潜能和自己的能力建设一个更美好的世界。这是有史以来最好的时代，无论你选择如何对待自己的生活，也无论你将自己的激情燃烧在哪里。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">No generation has ever held more power than yours. And no generation has been able to make change happen faster than yours can. The pace at which progress is possible has accelerated dramatically. Aided by technology, every individual has the tools, potential, and reach to build a better world. That makes this the best time in history to be alive. Whatever you choose to do with your life…Wherever your passion takes you.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p style='text-align: center;outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans sans-serif;text-align: justify;'>I won't let you down.   </span></strong></p><p style='text-align: center;outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 0px;color: rgb(9, 9, 9);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">There's something I never told you, Kate.有件事我一直没告诉你。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You see, it was my father who built the lake house.湖畔小屋是家父盖的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I mean, with his own hands.他亲手盖的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">And it was a long time ago, before he was famous...很久以前，早在他成名之前，</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...when he still had a family and worshipped my mother.当时他还很顾家，深爱我母亲。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Her name was Mary, and the house was a gift for her.她叫玛丽，那栋房子是送她的礼物。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She was smart and funny.她聪明又风趣。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1____________________________________________.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You see, the more successful he became, the more impossible he was to live with.他愈是成功就愈难和他共处同一屋檐下。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Finally, she just couldn't take living with him anymore.最后，她受不了和他一起生活。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She left him.她离开他了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Within a year, she got sick.不到一年，她就病倒了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Unfortunately, she never learned how to stop loving him.很遗憾她始终无法停止爱他。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He wasn't at the funeral.他没出席葬礼。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">When I asked him why...我问他为什么没去…</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Go on, Alex. What did he say?继续啊，他怎么说？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2____________________________________.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">And then he gave me one of his architect-of-the-year grins.然后他对我露出年度风云建筑师的招牌笑容。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top:
